The Federation of Labor Unions Replies to the Asian Labor Conference Stating: - Promote the Desire for International Peace - Uphold Justice Based on the Purpose of the Conference - The Unprecedented Crisis in East Asia Can Be Resolved

The Second Asian Labor Conference will be held in Japan starting on April 8th of next year. The conference sent a letter to the branch of the International Labor Bureau, which forwarded it to the Municipal Federation of Labor Unions, requesting that it send representatives to attend at that time. After receiving the letter, the Municipal Federation of Labor Unions submitted it to the Standing Committee for discussion. They all believed that the nature of the meeting was worth studying before Sino-Japanese relations were adjusted. Therefore, it was decided to inquire first and state the desire to promote international peace. The original letter is as follows: "To the esteemed colleagues, We have just received your letter stating that the Second

Asian Labor Conference

has been rescheduled to April 8, 9, and 10 of next year (1937) and will still be held in Japan. Please send representatives to participate at that time. A communication address is attached, and we are instructed to reply directly. We approve of the convening of the Asian Labor Conference and sincerely hope to send representatives to attend and join your association to seek happiness for Asian workers. However, the organization of your association is just beginning, and the environment is harsh, making it impossible for us to participate. We believe that the rampant imperialism, the tyranny of the capitalist class, the inequality of various treatments, and the instability of international peace make it necessary for all labor unions to unite and stand on the same front in order to improve the lives of workers and promote equality and the realization of peace. Furthermore, according to Article 2, Item 8 of your association's constitution, 'The purpose is to avoid war, establish international peace,

resist enemies of the state

and capitalism,' which coincides with our association's propositions. In addition to admiring it, we sincerely hope to join your association and jointly assume the responsibility of promoting social justice and international peace. However, looking back at the position of our country's workers today, they are subjected to the aggression of imperialism and the oppression of capitalists. The foundation of international peace has been destroyed by those with strong forces. Foreigners in China, under the cover of unequal treaties, have caused the Shanghai Concession Factory Inspection Agreement to fail. Those with ambitions are again

encouraging smuggling in North China

causing our industry and commerce to be on the verge of bankruptcy, workers' unemployment is increasing day by day, and life is becoming increasingly precarious. Our country's workers are oppressed by this cruel environment at home and have no recourse to appeal. Abroad, they are subjected to unequal treatment and are exiled back to the country one after another. We believe that this situation has long been understood by your association. Because your association aims to avoid war, establish international peace, resist imperialism and capitalism, and abolish the aggression suffered by workers in Asian countries under foreign influence, we deeply hope that your association will use democratic and recognized trade union methods to seek to carry out these goals. If, like the International Federation of Trade Unions and other international organizations that sympathize with labor, we can adopt the same policies and methods to promote justice for the loud appeals of the invaded, so as to promote social equity and

maintain world peace

then the unprecedented crisis in East Asia can be gradually resolved. If this is the case, not only can the goals that your association has embraced be fully realized, but the Asian labor front will also be increasingly consolidated. At that time, our association will not wait to be invited to participate and will naturally follow from the ground up, so as to promote the infinite welfare of Asian trade unions and workers. We have responded accordingly to the previous letter. We hope that you will review and provide clarification. Sincerely, the Shanghai Municipal Federation of Trade Unions to the Asian Labor Conference."

The Banking Association Held an Executive Committee Meeting Yesterday - Decided to Form an Income Tax Subcommittee - Recommended the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications as Members - Designated the Bank of China as the Convener of the Subcommittee

The Shanghai Banking Association held its 15th Executive Committee meeting yesterday afternoon at the Association's office on Hong Kong Road. Committee members Chen Guangfu, Wu Yunzhai, Yang Jemei, Zhuang Dezhi, Luo Qinghua, Qi Yunqing, Qu Jigang, Hu Xixian, Wu Weiru, Li Fuxun, Pan Jiufen, Zhang Peishen, and others attended. Secretary-General Lin Kanghou attended as an observer. Chen Guangfu presided over the meeting, and Gu Chengan recorded the minutes. First, the chairman reported that the Ministry of Finance has approved the association's request to postpone the implementation of the savings interest income tax until January 1st of next year. Now, the Income Tax Affairs Office has sent a letter instructing all banks to prepare everything so that it can be implemented as scheduled. All banks have been notified of this. Regarding the procedures for researching income tax collection, the Banking Society, local banking associations, member banks, and other organizations have all been asked to provide as much feedback as possible. This association has compiled it, and the Executive Committee meeting was specially convened today to seek public resolution. It was decided on the spot to organize a research income tax subcommittee, recommending 15 banks, including the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Bank of Shanghai, the National Goods Bank, the Guohua Bank, the Continental Bank, the Zhongnan Bank, the Yanye Bank, the Jincheng Bank, the Siming Bank, the Zhonghui Bank, the China Reclamation Bank, the China Agriculture and Industry Bank, the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, and the Zhejiang Xingye Bank, as members, and designated the Bank of China as the convener. The Banking Society's first research opinions, second research opinions, and the opinions of local banking associations and member banks were all submitted to the subcommittee for research. In addition, regarding the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's letter requesting the promotion of a "One-Day Donation" campaign for machine contributions, it was resolved to notify member banks to comply uniformly. Regarding the 1937 member bank holiday schedule, it was resolved to pass it. All member banks will take holidays according to this schedule. The meeting adjourned at 3:00 PM. As for the date of the first resolution meeting of the subcommittee, Secretary-General Lin said yesterday that it would be held after the 15 banks had nominated a committee and the Bank of China had convened it.

Japanese - Textile Factory Workers Endured the Pain and Resumed Work - The Government Will Properly Mediate Some of the Conditions - Workers at the Second Factory of the Public University Resumed Work Last Night - The Sixth Factory of the Shanghai West Inner and Outer Cotton Textile Factory Struck Again

The Dagong News Agency reported that all male and female workers of the Japanese-owned Shanghai and other textile factories in the Pudong area, after being persuaded by party and government agencies, endured the pain and resumed work in yesterday's day and night shifts. In the Shanghai West area, labor disputes occurred at the Japanese-owned Nei Wai Cotton, Xihe, and other textile factories. The details are recorded separately as follows:

Pudong Area - Resumption of Work Yesterday

At 5:30 AM yesterday morning, the Japanese-owned textile factories that had been on strike sounded the siren for Japanese workers to start work, and sent foremen and cooks to the workshops and workers' residences to coerce workers to enter the factory and resume work through intimidation and enticement. Fearing that disturbances would occur when workers resumed work, the factory notified the Yulin Road and Geland Road police stations and dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to patrol the area in advance to prevent them. Detectives were also stationed inside the factory. When the Japanese workers left work, most of the night workers were unwilling to go to work. After being earnestly persuaded by personnel sent by the Municipal Party Department, the Social Bureau, and the General Labor Union, they all resumed work. When the workers went to work, they were in groups of three or five. Some of the female workers were in tears, and some were pounding their chests and sighing, and the situation was very miserable.

Number of People Surveyed

The Dagong News Agency reporter went to various factories to investigate the number of workers who had resumed work. It was found that only 70% to 80% had resumed work. The details are recorded below:

Conditional Issues

Regarding the five requirements jointly proposed by the workers, the personnel department director of the Shanghai Spinning and Weaving Co., Ltd., Makino Naka, told the Dagong News Agency reporter yesterday that the factory had accepted the increase of 5% in wages and improved the working conditions for workers. As for other conditions, such as awards, they would try to improve them when the factory's situation improved in the future. According to the worker representatives of the factory, after the joint strike of the workers in various factories, they originally hoped that the factory would give a satisfactory answer to the conditions proposed by all the workers. Unexpectedly, things went against their wishes and they could not achieve their goals. Under the pressure of life, the workers had to endure the pain and resume work, but they hoped that the government authorities would plan for a proper solution to the conditions proposed by the workers.

Call for Interrogation

The Municipal Social Bureau summoned workers' representatives from various Japanese-owned textile factories at 10:00 AM yesterday morning. Fifteen workers' representatives attended, and the director of the mediation section, Wang Xianqing, personally inquired the workers' representatives one by one. Because the Japanese Textile Industry Association in China was scheduled to respond to the workers' five conditions yesterday morning, the Japanese side still had no news to the Bureau by 12:00 noon, so there was no way to discuss it. However, the Bureau informed the representatives of the factories and persuaded the workers to wait quietly for mediation. The representatives returned at 0:30 AM.

Public University Resumes Work

The second factory of the Japanese-owned Public University Textile Factory in Badaitou, Yangshupu, has resumed work after all workers responded to the strike on the morning of the 12th. At 6:00 PM last night, the factory dispatched staff and foremen to notify the night shift male and female workers to enter the factory. The personnel department director, Kawase, gave a speech in the open space in front of the factory workshop for half an hour, allowing the workers to increase their wages by 5%, so the night shift workers resumed work uniformly at 7:35 PM.

Shanghai West Area - The Sixth Factory of Nei Wai Cotton Struck

The entire workforce of more than 800 male and female workers at the Sixth Factory of Nei Wai Cotton on Yichang Road in Shanghai West went on strike on the night shift of the 12th because a female worker in the yarn room was beaten by the Japanese supervisor, which led to the departure of all the male and female workers from the factory and a strike. Then, the workers also proposed four conditions, including increasing wages. The factory workshop manager, Nakano Kayohei, asked the general foreman, Katsuta, for instructions, but there was no response, causing all the workers to continue the strike yesterday. In addition, the Eighth Factory of Nei Wai Cotton on Gordon Road also experienced a go-slow strike due to the dismissal of workers, and the dispute has not yet been resolved.

The Xihe Textile Factory - Also Proposes Conditions

All workers in the First, Second, and Third Factories of the Japanese-owned Xihe Textile Factory on Robertson Road have jointly proposed six conditions, including wage increases, weekly promotions, and monthly awards (the content of which is the same as in the Pudong area), and requested them from the factory. The factory has not yet responded, and the workers' emotions are agitated. It is not known whether a labor dispute can be avoided.

Shipping Industry Developing - Yangtze River Shallow Water Worrisome - Changsha Water Level Drops to One Foot - Freight Rates Rise by 125% - Salt and Coal Transportation Obstructed

Recently, the Yangtze River has seen more exports than imports, and transfers to Hunan Province are even more crowded. However, the Xiang River's water level has dropped sharply, causing a recent telegram from Changsha to state that only one foot of water remains above the Lulin Pond. Ships traveling from Shanghai to Hunan can only reach Yuezhou and then have to transfer cargo. The freight rate for this route has already risen by 75% at the Six Companies. Now, because Dongting Lake cannot be navigated by wheels and the waterway is completely cut off, only civilian boats and shallow barges can barely sail. Therefore, the Six Companies continued to discuss and increased the shallow water fee by 50%, bringing the total increase to 125%. Since the beginning of Changsha shipping, the magnitude of the freight rate has been unprecedented. In the past few decades, the highest freight rate only increased by 80%. The shallowest point in the Jiujiang area is 13 feet 6 inches. All seagoing vessels with a draft of more than 14 feet are difficult to pass through. The seagoing vessels transporting salt from Haizhou have a draft of at least 17 feet and will now be blocked. Kangshou Company's Chang'an wheel telegraphed yesterday that it was stranded on the river surface four miles below Wuxue while loading coal from Tongzibao to Shanghai. The company sent an empty wheel Ruikang in Han to rescue, but the wheel has a draft of 18 feet and could not go. They had to send a barge to unload the cargo before trying to rescue it.

Shallow Water Difficult to Navigate

This has caused the salt freight rate to rise from 4 yuan 7 corners to 7 yuan 5 corners, and the coal ton price to rise from 2 yuan 2 corners to 3 yuan 5 corners, but there are still no ships to load. In past years, the Yangtze River's water level has consistently dropped between January and early April, called the dry season. This year, however, the water level has already dropped to a point where navigation is difficult in October. According to observations in the shipping industry, during the dry season in December and January in the future, the water level is likely to drop to the starting point of the current water level gauge. At that time, none of the Shanghai Six Companies wheels will be able to navigate. The general Hakka community is also very worried and is discussing changing to

Railway Transfer

The method is to transfer the downstream cargo from the Pinghan Railway to the Longhai Railway and take the sea route to Shanghai. The upstream cargo from Shanghai is loaded onto the Lianyungang and transferred to the Longhai Railway to connect with the Pinghan train. This way, cargo transportation will not be interrupted, but the freight rate will be higher. As for the Xiaochang River (i.e., the Shanghai section of the Tongyang River), this year, due to the abundant harvests of miscellaneous grains and cotton in the areas north of the Yangtze River, there is a lot of stockpiling waiting to be loaded onto Shanghai. This route was originally traveled by ships of the Dada and Datong companies. Now, due to the crowding of cargo, the original eight wheels are insufficient to supply the demand. It is said that the two companies have agreed to increase the number of flights and expand the transportation capacity. They have already leased the Yongan wheel of the Dazhen Shipping Company and the Tianshi wheel of the Chongming Shipping Company to join the route. It is expected that additional flights will be added on the 15th of this month.

Wang Jun’s Family in Shanghai, Yesterday Departed for Shaanxi for Funeral; Wang Left Behind Three Sons and One Daughter; Wang Has an Elderly Mother Currently in Yunnan

Wang Jun, the army commander of the Central Third Army, recently led his troops in suppressing communist bandits in eastern Gansu. On the ninth, while taking the opportunity of a lull in the fighting to inspect the front lines, his plane crashed and burned, resulting in his death. Mr. Wang's family resides in Shanghai. The Shenzhou News Agency reporter visited Wang's residence at Lane 1136, Yuyuan Road, yesterday to inquire. According to his family, the news of Mr. Wang's accident in the line of duty was only relayed by the Nanjing Third Army Office on the eleventh. At that time, it was only stated that the plane had crashed, and the true details were unknown. Yesterday morning, a long-distance phone call from the capital confirmed Mr. Wang's death in eastern Gansu. Mrs. Xia, Mr. Wang's wife, was deeply saddened upon hearing the news. She immediately departed for Beijing by car at 1 p.m. yesterday, accompanied by several other family members, to meet with Director Shi of the Third Army's Beijing Office and proceed to Shaanxi for the funeral. Mr. Wang left behind three sons and one daughter. All three sons are studying in Beijing, and the daughter is in Shanghai. She has already accompanied Mrs. Wang to Shaanxi and will proceed to Pingliang to handle the funeral arrangements. Mr. Wang has an elderly mother currently in Yunnan. Mr. Wang's father passed away early. It is also learned that when Mr. Wang's plane crashed, two pilots also perished at the same time, making a total of three casualties including Mr. Wang.

Qian Junrui Returned to China Yesterday to Promote the Peace Movement

Qian Junrui, who went abroad to investigate the European economy and attend the World Peace Congress in Brussels, returned to China on the French postal ship Fèlix Roussel. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday. According to Mr. Qian, he originally intended to go to the United States from Europe to continue his investigation, but he was entrusted by Sir Cecil, the president of the World Peace Congress, and Mr. Guthe (French Minister of Aviation) to return to China urgently to promote the peace movement. He planned to report on the proceedings of the congress and its development plan, so he immediately changed his itinerary and returned to his motherland. Mr. Qian also said that more and more leaders from all walks of life in China are supporting the world peace movement. Therefore, the leaders of the congress are very impressed with the enthusiasm of the Chinese people for the peace movement. After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Qian plans to visit dignitaries in Beijing and Shanghai to convey Sir Cecil's gratitude and discuss concrete ways to promote the peace movement in China.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables Ministry of Finance to Request Reduction in Price of Henan Sulphur

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a cable to the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, which reads: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: On the eleventh of this month, we received a letter from Dazhong Dyeing Co., Ltd., stating that sulphur is one of the main raw materials of our factory. Since the government ordered the use of sulphur produced in Henan, we have repeatedly contacted the Henan Nitrate and Sulphur Bureau. Initially, we had to give up because the sulphur was not suitable for dye production. Later, after the Henan sulphur was refined, samples were sent, and after testing, it seemed to be usable. However, the price was too high, exceeding the ordinary market price by more than 60%. With such a large disparity, it is difficult to approach. Although we have repeatedly requested the bureau to refer to the current market price and make a reasonable adjustment, the Henan sulphur clearly knows this but refuses to reduce the price due to cost considerations. However, the government has ordered the use of Henan sulphur, and we must comply with the order, but we cannot help but speak out. The government's promotion of the state-run sulphur business is not something we dare to criticize. However, on the one hand, the Henan sulphur refuses to set prices based on market conditions, and on the other hand, our factory cannot but comply with the order to use Henan sulphur. Under these circumstances, we can only abandon the principal and seek the secondary. We appeal to the government to waive the freight charges for the Henan sulphur as a remedy. (Omission) Our dyeing industry is in the trial stage, with our factory being the earliest, and our products having only three or four years of history. Among all the companies in the industry, including Zhongfu, Huaan, and our factory, Zhongfu, the largest in terms of capital, has collapsed repeatedly due to the pressure of foreign goods and has finally ceased operations. Our factory and Huaan are still struggling to survive, and the difficulty of the current situation is self-evident. The sales volume of domestic dyes on the market is less than one-tenth of that of foreign goods, which is inversely proportional to the sales of matches. However, foreign merchants still regret that we have not been defeated, and Japanese merchants are actively setting up factories to manufacture dyes in Shanghai. According to current investigations, there are already three factories producing dyes. These three Japanese factories certainly need to use sulphur, but it is a fact that they have not purchased Henan sulphur to date. In contrast, if our factory bears the special price of Henan sulphur and cannot compete with Japanese goods, it will be even more obvious. We have investigated and found that Henan sulphur is a domestic product, and it is our duty to promote its purchase. However, the price is 60% higher than the market price, causing our factories to lose as much as 10,000 yuan per year in raw materials. This is tantamount to the state-run nitrate factory forcing contributions, which is not in line with trade norms. If a loss of 10,000 yuan is not significant, now that one of the three Chinese factories has closed, and the three factories set up by foreign merchants in Shanghai are not subject to mandatory use of Henan nitrates, the cost of raw materials is the key to the survival of manufacturers. This request for price reduction is an urgent appeal for self-help, not a petty calculation. As for the situation of match factories, because domestic factories have decades of history and a solid foundation, they cannot be compared with dye factories, as the factory's original text has stated, without the need for further elaboration. Based on the above reasons, we should cable your ministry to request a review and approval, and order the Kaifeng Nitrate and Sulphur Refinery in Henan to sell at the same price, in order to achieve a win-win situation for both people and ourselves. Otherwise, if these factories become the successors of Zhongfu, Henan nitrates may not benefit from trade either. It is important to plan comprehensively, pay attention to near-term interests, and turn them into a disservice. We are eagerly awaiting your instructions. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully submits this."

Chamber of Commerce Sends Letter to French Municipal Council to Improve Production of Vehicle Licenses

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to the French Concession Municipal Council, which reads: "To the esteemed Council: On the eleventh of this month, we received a letter from the Municipal Rickshaw Industry Association, stating that the rickshaw licenses in the French Concession have always been made by prisoners. The procedures for pasting and oiling are completely perfunctory, resulting in the paper and lead sheet of the license being broken and torn apart within a few days after the rickshaw merchant pays the business tax, and then peeling off completely. The rickshaw merchant then writes the original number on it, but the patrol often refers to it as confused business, and pries off the license, causing the rickshaw merchant and rickshaw puller to suffer unexpected losses innocently. If the license is pried off for other reasons, the license paper is lost, and the rickshaw puller cannot redeem it with a good piece of paper, so he has to stop business and wait, and the loss is even more unbearable. In addition, the Revenue Office requires the rickshaw merchant to submit the old license every month. For licenses with only the lead sheet left, the revenue office will not issue a donation certificate and will stop issuing licenses unless the association proves it and replenishes the lead. This is not the fault of the rickshaw merchant, but the rickshaw merchant has suffered losses again and again. The association has sent a letter to the Electricity Bureau requesting improvement, but no improvement has been seen. For this reason, we have poured out our feelings, and we urge your council to send a letter to the French Concession Municipal Council to promptly find a way to improve the production of the rickshaw licenses, so that the rickshaw merchant's expenses can be used for business for one month, and not suffer other losses due to the peeling off of the license paper. Before a solution is found, please stop withholding licenses and submitting old licenses. Although this is a trivial loss, it has a great impact on the rickshaw industry. We urge you to strive for rectification in order to live up to the expectations of the industry and maintain commercial prosperity. The association has investigated and found that the license paper is pasted on the lead sheet, which is easy to break and cannot be used for one month of business. If the patrol sees the number and the handwriting is slightly ambiguous, they will pry off the license. When going to redeem the license, there are also difficulties and additional fees, which is very obstructive to the rickshaw puller's business and should be improved. It is necessary to improve it. We should inform your office to promptly instruct the Vehicle Affairs Office to properly improve the various points mentioned in the letter. We hope to hear from you soon."

Progress of the Preparatory Committee of the Songjiang Fellow Association

The Songjiang Fellow Association in Shanghai, after the accumulation of efforts by Shanghai natives from the county, including Cheng Kaixian, Geng Jizhi, Ma Yinliang, Zhang Xiaotong, Cai Bubai, and others, has now rented No. 1 Wubenfang, Caishi Road, Avenue Lafayette, French Concession as the association's address. The preparatory committee has begun to arrange it and has scheduled the second preparatory meeting at the new association address at 5:00 p.m. on the 18th of this month (Wednesday). At the same time, the association has been actively seeking members in recent days. The methods are as follows: (1) The association has temporarily hired 100 captains of solicitation teams; (2) Each captain of the team must solicit at least 10 members; (3) The solicitation time is from November 1, 25th year of the Republic to December 31st; (4) The captain is the introducer of the member and is responsible for collecting the first membership fee and joining fee on behalf of the member; (5) The solicitation method is based on scores: each permanent member is 20 points, and each ordinary member is 1 point. The solicitation results of each solicitation team captain are proportional to the number of points. If the results are excellent, the conference will make and present souvenirs as rewards. It is learned that the captains hired by the association, in addition to the initiators who are natural captains, other captains of the solicitation teams have requested to be captains on their own initiative, which shows the eager expectations of the Shanghai natives of the county for the association.

Shanghai Rotary Club Issues Hospital Lottery Tickets to Raise Funds to Build Children's Convalescent Hospital

The Shanghai Rotary Club has always been committed to serving the society and running various charitable undertakings. It is extremely concerned about the poor children in this city. For example, the summer outings and entertainment for poor children and the distribution of toys to poor children during the Christmas season in winter are all collected from various Chinese and Western elementary schools and specially repaired. In recent years, a total of more than 26,000 pieces have been donated. The poor children who receive the donations are mostly between the ages of eight and eighteen. This year, in order to raise funds for the construction of a children's convalescent hospital for the poor (a part of Zhongshan Hospital), in addition to holding a charitable boxing competition, which has already raised more than 3,000 yuan, more than 20,000 yuan is still needed. Therefore, it was decided to issue one-yuan lottery tickets and authorize major companies and stores to sell them on their behalf. The first prize for each ticket is a Chevrolet car worth 4,000 yuan, the second prize is an electric refrigerator worth 800 yuan, the third prize is a receiver worth 500 yuan, and there are many other prizes. It is hoped that people from all walks of life will actively purchase tickets, both to help charity and win huge prizes. Also, tomorrow (15th) at 10:00 a.m., the Great Shanghai Grand Theatre will voluntarily welcome children to watch a movie for a fixed fee. The method is that each child who goes to watch the movie must bring a broken toy at home to enter the venue.

Silver Prices Gradually Stabilizing; Equalization Tax Rate Reduced

The Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee, jointly formed by the Central Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, had successively increased the equalization tax rate to prevent the export of silver due to the soaring international silver prices. It was 15.6% on the 10th and 21.25% on the 11th, breaking the highest record since autumn. The 12th was the anniversary of the Prime Minister's birthday, and there was no market due to the holiday. It is now learned that the committee believes that world silver prices have stabilized, so yesterday the Central Bank of China's listed equalization tax rate has been reduced to 9.5%, which has restored the original tax rate of 10 days ago.

Social Bureau Reiterates Crackdown on Disguised Escort Agencies; Establishing Names to Harm Society; Deadline for Dissolution or Severe Punishment

Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, previously issued a public notice banning escort agencies in this city because they were related to local morals and customs, and prohibited them from publishing advertisements in newspapers. However, it did not take long for all escort agencies to change their names one after another and still try to exist. Director Pan of the Bureau has once again banned them in order to rectify public morals. A public notice was issued yesterday, stating: "Recently, escort agencies in this city have been established everywhere. After careful investigation, most of them are using names as a pretext to carry out seduction. After this Bureau banned newspapers from publishing their advertisements, there were also disguised organizations such as dance partner agencies, tour guide agencies, and service agencies. Such clever establishment of names to harm society, if not strictly prohibited, how can we maintain morals and maintain law and order? Therefore, this special public notice is given to all, urging all escort agencies and various disguised organizations to dissolve within a deadline. If they still act contrary to the ban, they will be severely punished according to law."

Public Concession Factory Accidents Last Month

According to a report from the Shanghai Municipal Council's Factory Section, a total of 203 industrial and occupational accidents occurred in the Public Concession during October, resulting in three deaths. Fourteen women were injured. The causes of 197 incidents were generally clear. Investigations were conducted, and methods for prevention and aftercare were provided in 114 cases.

Analyzing the causes of these dangerous incidents, 50 were related to electrical machinery. Among these, one person died in an elevator accident, and five were injured by electric shock, with no fatalities. Six people were burned by fire, with no deaths. Four people were burned by hot and corrosive materials. Three were injured by toxic gases. Twenty-six people were injured by falling from heights. Twenty-two were injured by falling objects. Eighteen were injured in collisions, including one death.

Breaking down the incidents by industry type, the machinery and metal manufacturing industries had the most accidents, with 47 cases, fortunately without any fatalities. The building construction industry had 13 cases, including one death. The textile industry had 34 cases, with no deaths. The transportation industry had 29 cases, including one death. The printing industry had 11 cases, with no deaths.

Health Department Declares No Plague in the Concession

A recent report stated that the plague had recently occurred in the Public Concession of Shanghai, with several casualties among residents. The Shanghai Municipal Council's Health Department has organized plague prevention teams in various districts within the Concession to prevent its spread and engage in catching rodents, etc. According to the person in charge of the Municipal Council's Health Department, the above report is completely inaccurate and believes that such rumors can easily cause panic among residents and disrupt public order within the Concession, so it is necessary to correct it. The responsible person added that the Public Concession has not had any plague cases in recent decades, and the Health Department's epidemic prevention team is actually an old organization that specializes in assisting residents in searching and catching rodents in various parts of the Concession. In addition, whenever dead rats are found, they are sent to the Municipal Council's laboratory for testing to check the possibility of the plague's existence. In the future, if residents in the Concession encounter matters related to public health, they can inquire with the Health Department at any time, so that the truth can be easily understood, and the public will not be alarmed by false rumors.

Shanghai Municipal Council Plans to Cut Staff and Salaries, Chinese Employees' Association Held General Meeting Yesterday, Over 600 People Unanimously Oppose

Due to the economic downturn in recent years, which has affected various tax revenues, the Shanghai Municipal Council has been unable to reduce expenditures and has formed an Employee Economic Committee to propose salary cuts and layoffs. The Chinese Employees' Association of the Council held a general meeting of members at Gezhi Public School yesterday afternoon at 6 p.m., with over 600 people attending. Zhu Lianxiang chaired the meeting and reported the purpose of the meeting. Subsequently, Special Committee Member Zhang Jusheng reported on the progress of the research. After discussion, it was unanimously stated that if layoffs and salary cuts are to be implemented, Chinese employees must be treated the same as foreign employees. It was also decided to authorize the Executive Committee to negotiate with the Council. All proposals must be submitted to the association within four days for negotiation. At the same time, an official statement was issued opposing salary cuts. After the Council officially announces the measures, another general meeting will be held to discuss countermeasures.

Gao Yongxing Velvet Weaving Factory Fire Yesterday Morning Claims Seven Lives, Caused by Electric Motor Igniting Fluff During Napping Process, Same Type of Fire Has Occurred Three Times in the Past Year, Social Affairs Bureau and Municipal Council Send Personnel for Detailed Investigation

The Gao Yongxing Velvet Weaving Factory at No. 13, Alley 172, Ala Baisituo Road, North Zhejiang Road, suddenly caught fire at 1 a.m. yesterday morning, burning seven workers to death. The Factory Inspection Office of the Third Section of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Factory Section of the Public Concession Municipal Council have sent personnel to investigate in detail. The estimated loss is 50,000 yuan. Details are as follows:

Spreading to Neighbors

The Gao Yongxing Velvet Weaving Factory suddenly caught fire at 1 a.m. yesterday morning. The night shift was still in progress, and seven day-shift workers were sleeping in the building. The building was an old-style shop with several looms and napping machines inside. Of the seven people sleeping in the building, four were sleeping on the upper floor of the combing machine, and the remaining three were sleeping in the rear room downstairs. After the fire broke out, the four people upstairs could not escape while sleeping and were all burned to death. Of the three downstairs, two were burned to death. One of them, after escaping, went back into the fire and suddenly collapsed and died. Fortunately, the West District Fire Brigade dispatched vehicles to put out the fire and, together with the factory's shift workers, made every effort to extinguish it. However, because the fire was too fierce, it spread to the Tongjihe Wine Shop at No. 11 and a certain surname's residence at No. 9. It was not completely extinguished until about 10 a.m. However, Nos. 13 and 15, the factory, were completely destroyed.

Seven Lives Lost

After the incident, the West District Fire Brigade found the bodies of seven day-shift workers burned to death in the rubble. A letter was sent to the coroner's office. The names of the people burned to death are as follows: (1) Zhao Zhixiang, 42 years old; (2) Shao Longgen, 30 years old; (3) Zhang Shunji, 22 years old; (4) Qian Liansheng, 27 years old; (5) Yang Lisheng, 23 years old; (6) Shao Fugeng, 28 years old; (7) Zhou Amao, 40 years old. The factory's loss is estimated at 50,000 yuan. As for the losses of the neighboring Tongjihe Wine Shop and a certain surname's residence, they are not included.

Cause of the Fire

After receiving the report, the Factory Section of the Public Concession Municipal Council immediately sent personnel to the factory to investigate the cause and process of the fire in detail. According to the information released by the Information Office, the Factory Section personnel of the Municipal Council investigated the workers at the scene afterward and learned that the fire was caused by the fluff on the electric motor being ignited by electricity. Because the combing machine emits fine fluff when combing the wool, it flies onto the electric motor and is easily burned. It was also found that the same type of fire had occurred three times in the past year, but fortunately, there were no loss of life. Therefore, the Factory Section of the Municipal Council has paid special attention to this matter and recently went to 15 weaving factories to investigate. Gao Yongxing Factory had been inspected once on October 9. At that time, the factory's air circulation was considered good, and the wool could be extracted at any time during the combing process, so it would not fly into the workshop. The other six factories did not have such equipment. Since then, only one factory has installed this complete equipment in accordance with the regulations.

Authorities Investigate

After receiving the report, the Factory Inspection Office of the Third Section of the Social Affairs Bureau immediately sent factory inspectors Tian Heqing and others to the scene to investigate in detail. It is reported that the factory employs more than 120 workers, working in two shifts, day and night. When the fire broke out yesterday morning, the day-shift workers had all left the factory, and the night-shift workers, about 50 people, were working and immediately escaped to the outside of the factory. However, the seven day-shift foremen, because they lived in the factory, were awakened in their sleep and could not escape, resulting in a tragic death by fire.

Settlement Plan Agreed for the July-August Cotton Flower Dispute, Brokerage Association Subsidizes 190,000 Yuan, Exchange Assists with 230,000 Yuan

Shenzhou News Agency reports that the Futures Exchange was previously a bull company organized by financial securities and other giants, with daily transactions exceeding one million. At that time, the total number of cotton flowers held reached a huge 17 to 18 million. Therefore, the cotton market rose higher and higher, but the current sales of yarn were sluggish, and the price of yarn fell miserably every day, causing difficulties for all factories. At the same time, the officials of the Futures Exchange believed that this speculative transaction would create great danger, so they stopped new transactions in accordance with the Exchange Law and could only settle transactions, resulting in huge losses of several million yuan for the company. They had no choice but to refuse delivery on the grounds of poor cotton quality. The losses suffered by the 13 agent brokers were therefore very large. Now, the board of directors of the Exchange and the Brokerage Association jointly bear the losses of the bull company and the 13 brokers. However, the board of directors of the Exchange is tight-lipped about the amount of compensation for the losses of the bull company. According to rumors in the industry, it is around 500,000 yuan and has already been allocated by the board of directors under special expenses. As for the losses of the 13 brokers, a proper solution has been reached, and all brokers are notified to comply. The bull company case of the number of disputes has come to an end. The announcement is recorded as follows: Announcement of the Futures Exchange Brokerage Association: Regarding the cotton flower dispute in July and August of this year, 15 members previously sent letters requesting a special meeting of all members to discuss solutions. On September 4, at 4:00 p.m., the association held a meeting of all members and elected Chairman Wu Kouqing, Vice Chairman Shao Wenmei, Vice Chairman Zhou Shaokang, Member Zhou Zixing, and Member Qian Hejin and five gentlemen represented by Sun Yufeng as representatives of the association to discuss methods with the Exchange to handle the case jointly. After the above five gentlemen represented the association and negotiated repeatedly with the Exchange, there was no other appropriate solution except for the following methods. The methods agreed upon by the representatives of the association and Ling Yisuo are listed below: (1) All members of the association will subsidize 190,000 yuan in national currency to the 13 members including Hexing, Jinchang, Taichang, Yichang, Runkang, Fengtai, Changfeng, Rongji, Shenji, Yuda Tongji, Senkang, Hu Meiji, and Mingde. This amount will be borrowed first by the association from the Exchange without interest. The method of repayment is that all members of the association and their successors will pay an additional subsidy of 2.5 cents per hundred from the new cotton flower transactions starting on December 1 of this year. Half will be paid if not paid in advance. Both will be collected by one party. The Exchange will collect it daily until 175,000 yuan is collected. The remaining 15,000 yuan will be paid by the association from the fund when the Exchange collects 175,000 yuan. (2) In addition to the aforementioned 190,000 yuan, the representatives of the association will also send a letter to the Exchange on behalf of all members, asking them to take into account the difficulties of the aforementioned 13 members and provide another 230,000 yuan in national currency to help them maintain their operations. (3) Regarding the 190,000 yuan in national currency borrowed from the Exchange, five representatives jointly elected by all members of the association should sign two copies of the agreement separately with the Exchange, each holding one copy as evidence. The above methods have been agreed upon by the representatives of the association and the Exchange and are hereby notified.

So, he stayed at his friend Chen Qi's place at the dead body number of Hengchang Lane, Peile Road. Now, the father-in-law has written a letter allowing the engagement to take place within a week and has submitted the evidence. Subsequently, Xi Yexian testified that she cohabitated with Hu under her parents' orders, and her testimony was the same as Hu's. The court investigated and ruled to reschedule the hearing for the 19th because the plaintiff was not present. Hu Zhuoxing was ordered to be escorted by Chen Qi, who would be responsible for his attendance.

Li Liejun and Others Initiate Public Burial for Martyr Qian Gang, All Sectors in Wujiang Have Formed a Preparatory Committee, Discussing Naming a "Digen Road" in Shanghai

Revolutionary martyr Qian Gang (Digen) was appointed Commander-in-Chief of the Jiangsu National Revolutionary Army in Shanghai, engaged in secret work when the Northern Expeditionary Army had not yet arrived in Shanghai in 1927. On the 16th of that month, he was arrested by Li Baozhang, subordinate of Sun Chuanfang, and martyred in Longhua. At that time, Qian's family escorted the remains back to their native Wujiang and temporarily placed them in the Reception Temple. More than nine years have passed since then, and he has not yet been buried. Court President Ju Zheng, Foreign Minister Zhang Qun, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Education Director Pan Gongzhan, Garrison Headquarters Military Law Office Director Lu Jingshi, Central Committee Member Li Liejun, Liu Yazi, Xue Dubi, Chu Minyi, and others had petitioned the National Government in 1920 to provide a public burial for Qian to comfort his spirit. Because the public burial regulations had not yet been promulgated that year, it was inconvenient to hold one. Now, it is learned that Li Liejun and others have revived the previous proposal to request an allocation of funds and arrange a public burial for Qian. At the same time, all sectors in Wujiang County are preparing to hold a grand tenth anniversary commemoration of Qian Gang's martyrdom on January 16 next year, build a memorial monument, and have formed the Wujiang All Sectors Public Burial Qian Gang Martyr Preparatory Committee. Representatives Jin Luwang were also sent to Shanghai, carrying letters to visit Shanghai Mayor Wu, asking for a road in Shanghai to be named Digen Road in memory of his meritorious deeds.

The weather in Shanghai has recently returned to mild, unlike winter. At the same time, dense fog has occurred for several consecutive days, greatly affecting transportation. The Datong News Agency reporter reports the situation as follows:

Amidst Strikes, Two Cases of Trouble Makers are Prosecuted, Female Teacher Arrested for Intentional Incitement, Liu Wanxing and Others Sentenced to Detention

Amid the strike wave at Japanese-owned yarn factories in Shanghai, a resolution may be possible after several days of negotiations between labor and management. The afternoon before yesterday, Yangshupu Tongxing Yarn Factory posted notices outside the factory advising workers to resume work. The factory workers surrounded the bulletin, forming a wall. At that time, Chen Lifan, a woman from Zhenjiang and a teacher at the night school affiliated with a certain elementary school on Seward Road, told the gathered female workers that the notice did not mention wage increases and that they should not resume work. 捲欵潛逃　郁文朝被逮　交運公司未註冊　自訴案依法駁回

Yu Wen Zhao arrested for absconding with funds. The transportation company was not registered. The private prosecution was legally dismissed.

Unexpectedly, on December 26 of last year, Yu secretly took the company's receipt book and successively collected accounts receivable from various customers, amounting to 7,575 yuan, and absconded with the funds. After the company discovered this, they reported to the French Concession Police to request an arrest and offered a reward of 400 yuan. Until the day before yesterday, Yu was recognized by an employee of the Jiaoyun Transportation Company at the Old North Gate, who turned him over to the police and brought him to the branch office. The French Concession Police sent detectives to transfer Yu to the station. Xu Shengfu of the Jiaoyun Transportation Company, entrusted lawyer Sun Zuji as his agent, and filed a private prosecution with the Second District Court based on Article 236 of the Criminal Law for occupational embezzlement, along with a related civil suit requesting a judgment to repay 7,535 yuan. According to the complaint, the court, yesterday morning, had Judge Chen Shuoying conduct a preliminary hearing in the First Criminal Court. The court held that the plaintiff's company was not registered with the Ministry of Industry of the National Government and therefore could not pursue a private prosecution under the law. The court then ruled in court that the case was not accepted and the accompanying civil suit was dismissed. The plaintiff was also advised to request the police to file a public prosecution. The defendant was ordered to remain in custody during the appeal period.

中英通航後　一澳人購直達票　二十六日由上海起飛　下月七日可飛抵倫敦

After direct flights between China and Britain begin, an Australian buys a direct ticket, departing from Shanghai on the 26th and arriving in London on the 7th of next month.

After the China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC) established a station in Hong Kong, direct flights between China and Britain became available. According to CNAC news, an Australian named Mr. Bell Chue has already purchased a direct flight ticket from Hong Kong to England. This is the first person to purchase a direct flight ticket after the opening of direct flights between China and Britain. Mr. Bell is a famous Australian businessman who recently arrived in Hong Kong from Australia and then traveled to Japan via Shanghai. He will arrive in Shanghai from Japan on the 26th of this month, take a CNAC plane to Hong Kong, and then take the "Dorado" from Hong Kong via Penang to London, arriving on December 7. Further, regarding the important documents between China and Britain concerning the opening of direct flights, the reporter learned the following: Dai Enji, general manager of CNAC, sent a letter to Mr. Coontz, Far East manager of British Airways, stating, "The first southbound flight arrived in Hong Kong on November 5th and returned to Shanghai from Guangzhou this morning. Everything went very smoothly. Without your rich experience and decisive leadership, this achievement would not have been possible. We are writing this small note to express our gratitude. It is particularly gratifying that the Dorado, which made the first flight between China and Britain yesterday, already had one passenger, as well as mail, etc... The opening of direct flights between China and Britain is tantamount to connecting the capitals of the two countries, and its result will surely promote friendship between China and Britain." Mr. Coontz's letter to Mr. Dai read, "I have just received your letter, and I am pleased to learn of everything. I am unworthy of your praise. We are very pleased to cooperate with your company this time. We also learned that someone has already purchased a direct ticket from Shanghai to London. This is a prelude to the enhancement of friendship between China and Britain."

本市國醫學會　前日會員大會　討論提案改選執監

The Shanghai National Medical Association held a general membership meeting the other day to discuss proposals and re-elect executives and supervisors.

The Shanghai National Medical Association held its 15th general membership meeting at the Lake Society at 2 p.m. the other day. More than 400 members attended. Li Hao from the Municipal Party Department, Zhou Hanmei from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Tao Jian from the Municipal Health Bureau, Shen Hefu from the National Medicine Association, Ding Zhongying from the National Medicine Branch, Xu Xiangren from the Shenzhou National Medical Association, Jiang Wenfang from the National Medical Association, Lu Shi'e from the Chinese National Medical Association, and more than 400 members attended. Ding Jiwan, Lu Shi'e, Dai Dafu, He Yunsheng, and Zhou Zhaonan served as the presidium. The chairman first reported on the purpose of the meeting, and then representatives from the party and government agencies delivered speeches. The following proposals were then discussed: (1) Holding an academic paper review; (2) Regarding the outstanding issue of opposing the new regulations of the French Concession, it should be handled urgently to benefit colleagues; (3) The Regulations for the Examination of Traditional Chinese Medicine promulgated by the Executive Yuan should be inquired of the municipal government on how to implement them to facilitate the registration of colleagues; (4) The association should have another organization to respond to the needs of the times in matters such as first aid and detoxification in response to the war; (5) Unifying drug names to avoid misleading patients; (6) The association should establish a library for members to borrow; (7) It is proposed to organize a National Medical Club to connect feelings and regulate physical and mental health; (8) If the medical works published by members are reviewed and considered applicable by the association, please provide assistance to encourage and promote academic research; (9) Holding academic lectures; (10) Efforts should be made to rectify national medicine and value human life; (11) It is recommended to establish a municipal Chinese medicine hospital; (12) Organizing a time epidemic relief team (Decision) The above cases were handed over to the next executive and supervisory committee for discussion and implementation. After the discussion, the executive and supervisory committees were elected. Due to lack of time, the list of elected candidates will be announced on the 15th. The meeting adjourned at about 5 p.m.

上海僑務局　遣送難僑回籍　旅荷旅日先後二批

The Shanghai Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau repatriates refugees to their hometowns in two batches from the Netherlands and Japan.

According to the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau, the recent situation of sending two batches of refugees back to their hometowns is recorded as follows:

Refugees from the Netherlands

Chen Yuli, a Chinese expatriate residing in the Netherlands, returned to China due to unemployment. After arriving in Shanghai, he ran out of travel expenses and could not speak the language. He was on the verge of destitution. The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Relief Section learned of his situation and transferred him to the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau. The bureau immediately sent him on the China Merchants Shipping Company's Haiheng ship to Shantou to transfer him to his hometown.

Refugees from Japan

The Japanese ship Asama Maru recently arrived in Shanghai with four deported refugees from Japan: Ye Ajiao, Zhou Kebian, Wen Wanjie, and Hu Jinxing. All of them worked in Japan for seven or eight years. Upon arrival in Shanghai, the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau sent personnel to the wharf to take care of them. As all of the refugees were from Yongjia, Zhejiang Province, they were sent on the China Merchants Shipping Company's Haiyan ship back to their hometowns.

中央銀行同人　假期旅行常熟

Employees of the Central Bank travel to Changshu during the holiday.

Employees of the Central Bank took advantage of the holiday on November 12, the anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's birth, to organize a tour to Changshu. More than 20 people, including Liu Fuzhong, Qian Xuanshou, Tang Yinshun, and Zhu Hanmin, joined the tour. Chen Jieliu and Shao Kuibin were elected as tour guides. At 7 a.m., they departed from the bank by car and arrived in Changshu at 9:30 a.m. They first visited the Weng Tonghe Prime Minister's Park, then climbed Yushan Mountain and visited Poshansi Temple, the place where Tang Changjian wrote his poem. The pool is now named Kongxin, taken from the meaning of the poem. Inside, there are Tang Gui and Song Mei trees. The Tang Gui still has lush branches and leaves, while the Song Mei is already withered. They then climbed Jianmen, the highest point of Yushan Mountain, with steep cliffs standing tens of feet tall, as if split by a divine axe into green and black cliffs. The top is sharp and the bottom is cut off, with a narrow gap in the middle that cannot accommodate the body, and it is dark and unpredictable. Both sides are huge rocks. Looking north to the sea and west to the lake, the sails, sand birds, and layered city buildings are all visible, making people linger and reluctant to leave. After the tour, they dined at the Shanjingyuan Restaurant. They left Changshu at 5 p.m. and arrived in Shanghai when the lights of thousands of homes were already lit.

Liu Xiaohu and Li argue over their daughter, with conflicting opinions.

Because their income is not enough to cover their expenses, the husband and wife each earn a living separately. Their three-year-old daughter is raised by a friend of Liu's. Recently, Liu's friend wanted to go elsewhere and asked him to take her back. It happened that Mrs. Zhang Wang, a native of Ningbo whom he knew well, wanted to adopt a daughter. Liu then gave his own daughter away, with both parties agreeing. Unexpectedly, Liu's wife, Li, refused, insisting that her husband was selling her. They argued in the city and were brought to the Yemiao Police Station for questioning.

Two fires occurred yesterday.

General Overview of Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Changes in July and August of This Year (Continued) (Thirty-eighth of the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview)

— Edited by China WeChat

(5) Changes in the branches of the World Book Company: Recently, after the twenty-two counties of eastern Hebei Province switched to using puppet textbooks, the business of the Tianjin branch plummeted, resulting in significant losses. Therefore, the board of directors decided to close the Tianjin branch and establish a new branch in Kaifeng. It is said that most of the inventory and original staff of the Tianjin branch were also transferred to the Kaifeng branch.

In July, the number of new retail businesses increased by two compared to the previous month, while the number of closures also increased by five compared to the previous month, indicating a continuing trend of decline from the previous month. The more important ones are briefly listed below:

(1) Li Yang Silk and Satin Store Closed: This store had been in business for over twenty years and was solely operated by Mr. Zhang Liehong. It was one of the major silk merchants in Shanghai. Its business was generally prosperous on ordinary days. However, recently, due to the market downturn and increasing competition among peers, it became difficult to maintain. On the first of this month, Mr. Zhang suddenly left with all the staff, and all goods and account books were also moved away, resulting in an informal bankruptcy.

(2) Tong Shun Silk Store Liquidation: This store had been open for over ten years. Previously, the owner of the store invested 1,000 yuan in the stock of the World Bank and simultaneously overdrawn over 1,100 yuan from the bank. After the World Bank ceased operations, the invested capital could not be recovered, but the overdraft had to be repaid urgently. Recently, the liquidator of the World Bank applied for seizure, forcing the store to close down.

(3) The Three Stores of Mr. Chu Qi Liquidation: Mr. Chu is the owner of the Maosheng He Qiji Tea and Leg Store on Nanjing Road, the Wang Wuting Tea Store on Route Cardinal Mercier, and the Tongfeng Maoji Leg Store in Xiaodongmen. The three stores' business was usually prosperous, with Maosheng He Qiji on Nanjing Road being the most successful, as it was located under the Letian Tea House and was a central hub of Shanghai traffic. The other two stores were also large in scale. In recent years, due to the impact of the economic downturn, business was slow, and economic turnover was difficult. On the 16th, the liquidation was announced simultaneously.

(4) Lao Fu Xing Shoe Store Liquidation: This store was established in 1927 with a capital of 3,000 national currency, solely founded by Mr. Liu Jiukang. Its business was usually quite stable. Recently, due to the market downturn, it repeatedly suffered losses and owed rent for as long as eight months. Therefore, the landlord, the Gongping Foreign Firm, sued in court, and the court executed the seizure, forcing the store to announce liquidation.

(5) World Industrial Company Business Closed: This company was solely founded by Mr. Wu Liegang, specializing in general merchandise. It also leased part of the store's space to other manufacturers to join in business. It had been in business for over two years. Recently, due to the sluggish market, poor business, competition from peers, and plummeting prices, as well as high rent and large expenses, economic turnover was difficult. Therefore, it had to announce liquidation.

(6) Opening of the Shanghai Antique Market: This market was initiated by over 500 antique dealers, expanding and relocating the original antique market at No. 74 Jiangxi Road. Currently, 70 companies have joined, making it the first large-scale antique market in Shanghai.

First Encounter Between Chinese and Western Heroes: Cai Huiquan Defeats Carson: Result 4-6, 6-4, 6-3

The tennis team of Shanghai University in Hongkou invited Carson, Cai Huiquan, Chen Runyuan, and Chen Qihao to the school yesterday for guidance and demonstration to improve their skills. The match between Carson and Cai was the most interesting. Both sides had skillful techniques and excellent postures. Although there were judgments of strength and weakness in physique, the techniques were comparable. However, Cai's backhand stroke was superior to Carson's, only the high pressure and serve were slower than Carson's. Yesterday's demonstration match was held at 2:30 PM. As a result of the toss, Cai served first. The first game was tied seven times, and finally Carson broke through. Cai also occupied Carson's serving game. Afterwards, Carson's momentum was quite strong and he won the first set with 6-4. In the deciding set, both sides won the game with the serve to make it 3-3. Then Carson went ahead 4-3. Cai took three games in a row to pull back the second set with 6-4. In the third set, Cai got the first game, and Carson chased to 1-1. Soon Cai made it 3-1, and Carson chased to 2-3. After Cai won two more games in a row, Carson only added one game. In the ninth game, Cai served. After two equalities, Cai went to the net to block and kill, and completed the great achievement with a light backhand cut, and defeated the stubborn Carson for a while with two to one, creating a good memory of the first encounter between the two. In the three sets, Carson attacked fiercely, while Cai used softness to overcome strength. Especially a few backhand slices and light blows on the baseline can be described as magical. After a short rest, Carson teamed up with Sun Yiqin, and Cai cooperated with Tang Baojia. This doubles match, Tang's group first won the first set with 6-4. Cai's group was repaid by Carson's group in the same way, each winning one. In the third set, Cai and Tang's group easily won again with 6-2, and then defeated Carson's group with two to one. At the same time, on the second court, Chen Runyuan, who had just returned from England, played a singles match with Tang Baojia. As a result, Chen won two games in a row with his superior skills. Then Chen cooperated with Chen Gonghao and played doubles against Kang Guangan and Sali Quan, the runner-up of Shanghai University. The strength of both sides was equal. Only one set was played, and it was dark and the game was over. Victory belonged to the two Chens, and the score was 11-9. The director of the school's sports department, American Professor Qi Hefu and his wife, hosted a tea party at their residence, and everyone dispersed in joy. The results of each group are as follows. Also, Cai and Chen Runyuan will go to Hangzhou at 3:00 PM this afternoon accompanied by Chen Qihao, return to Shanghai by night train tomorrow, and perform again in Fudan the day after tomorrow.

Tilden Talks About Tennis Methods: Li Huitang Records

The famous "William Tilden II" does not need me to introduce him. I believe that people who pay a little attention to tennis or understand world sports have a considerable understanding of him. This time, he and that young and handsome "Asheville Barnes" came to the East to perform their skills, stirring up the infinite excitement of East Asian tennis players. In the past, I read their achievements in newspapers or magazines, or sometimes caught a glimpse of their quick skills on the screen. I always felt a great regret that I could not be there to appreciate their superb skills in person. Today, we are still fortunate enough to have the opportunity to see their style in Hong Kong, and I am even more fortunate to be able to shake hands and talk with them.

At 6:30 PM on November 9, after the performance match between Tilden and Barnes, they gave a public speech in the Grand Terrace Garden of the Hong Kong Hotel. Hundreds of people gathered because of their reputation. In sixty minutes, Tilden talked about the scriptures, which were fascinating. He was still holding a racket in his hand, showing various grip methods, and sometimes demonstrating various hitting postures. His crane-shaped wide back, Ming Taizu-style chin, and authentic American voice were all materials that made people laugh, not to mention that he also mixed in humorous tones and humorous actions from time to time. He was not only a born tennis freak, but also a talented speaker. The following is a brief record of the main points of his talk:

General People's Mistakes

Many people have fundamentally wrong ideas, thinking that the game of tennis relies entirely on the movement of the hand holding the racket. In fact, this is a big mistake. Tennis is a thing that combines intelligence, eyesight, and body propulsion to achieve miraculous effects. The hand holding the racket is only responsible for the work of transmission. Also, the most important thing is the movement of the feet, which should be paid more attention to than the movement of the hands. If the pace is disordered, there will be few good performances. Ordinary people also have misunderstandings, thinking that the beginning and the end of tennis are the moment when the racket hits the ball. In fact, it has already started before the ball touches the racket, and it cannot be considered over even after the racket hits the ball.

Three Principles of Tennis

There are three basic principles of tennis. First, from the moment the ball is served until the ball dies, the eyes should be tightly focused on the ball, and the line of sight should be concentrated, and should not be shifted by the scenery outside the court. Although many players' eyes follow the ball, sometimes when the ball reaches their side, they raise their heads to observe the position of their opponents and forget to follow the ball with their eyes at the moment when the ball touches the racket, which sometimes causes the point of hitting the ball to not be in the center of the racket, which is not advisable for wise people. Top players do not need to observe the position of their opponents, because the secret of tennis lies in hitting the ball far away from the opponent's body, not hitting it next to the opponent's body, so that it is easier for them to return the ball. The second and third points are related, that is, when hitting the ball, you must turn your body and face the net sideways. It is difficult to have a good work if you hit the ball facing the net. When the racket hits the ball, the body should also have forward propulsion at the same time to increase the momentum of the ball. Therefore, beginners of tennis should have a deep understanding of these three points, and train their posture purely before taking a further step to seek hitting methods, otherwise the foundation is wrong, and it is difficult to have great gains.

The Most Important Hitting Method

Although there are many kinds of tennis hitting methods, the most important and most commonly used is the forehand stroke. If the forehand is not good, even if other hitting methods are excellent, it is difficult to hope to step onto the world stage. When stroking the ball, the left foot should be advanced, the body should face the net sideways, and wait for the ball to reach the height of the waist to meet it. If the ball comes too high, wait for it to fall to the same level as the waist before hitting it. If it is too low, you should bend your knees and squat down to hit it to match the steps. The backhand stroke has the same principles as the forehand stroke, only the left and right are switched. Serving is a thing that many people think is a medium for the ball game and ignore it. However, they do not know that serving is a sharp weapon for attack. Players should practice hard and not give up this right of attack. Although there are different types of serves, there are only two that are practical: one is the sliced ​​style, and the other is the American spin style. As for high-pressure balls, volley balls, cut balls, low passing balls, lobs, half volley balls, volley lobs, and all kinds of hitting methods, they all have their own value. However, when training hitting methods, you must first seek accuracy and then gradually increase the speed to achieve twice the result with half the effort.

Differences Between Men and Women

People often ask about the differences between men's and women's tennis. I think that due to the natural physical conditions of women, they are only suitable for baseline tactics and not suitable for net-front tactics. Men are different. In terms of physical strength, they are mainly based on baseline tactics, and in terms of mentality, they are mainly based on net-front tactics. Once there is an opportunity, they should go to the net to intercept and kill. Women's strength is not enough, and it is difficult to cope with them. As for those who are good at strokes, they must be able to beat those who are good at blocking the net. Experience and past achievements tell the truth. However, when meeting each other's long strokes and equal strength, those who are also good at defending the net must take advantage of it, there is no doubt.

Impressions of Listeners

After Mr. Tilden's speech was over, people in the audience asked about the difficult points, and he answered them one by one, which was quite interesting. Among them, there are many talks based on personal experience. In short, that one hour in the evening is deeply imprinted in people's minds, and it is recognized by people that it is not worth the trip. It is a pity that what he talked about that night were the basic principles and methods for beginners. Anyone who has read his book "Secrets of the Game and the Rebound of the Ball" knows that what he said this time is adding a little action, Chen Zhangzai's gift. He has played it through in that book. Most of the audience that night were people with a little tennis foundation and experience. He should have mixed his life experience and the more advanced mysteries of the game to guide them, which would be more interesting and valuable. However, no matter what kind of sport, it is impossible to improve in one day or one hearing and one lecture.

Tilden and Pan Lai

Many people mean that Tilden has a bit of a weird personality and his temper is different from ordinary people. His comments in writing or verbally are sometimes stubborn and prejudiced. Years ago, he saw the famous English player "Fulei Pan Lai" and said that his hitting method was wrong and it was difficult to achieve great things. Today, Mr. Pan is sitting high on the throne, and Mr. Tilden still does not change his old tune, and often says that the German king "Feng Gelinmu" is a better talent, so the British people are not very fond of Mr. Tilden, and there are often articles criticizing him in magazines and newspapers. But the benevolent sees benevolence, and the wise sees wisdom. Mr. Tilden may have other intentions. Perhaps he has a unique eye. Who can have an accurate and accurate judgment on right and wrong?

The Skills of Tilden and Van

These two days they performed in Hong Kong, it's really a feast for the eyes. Their speed and strength of serving, their composure in responding, their accuracy in long strokes, the beauty of their posture, and the regularity of their steps are not only unprecedented, I am afraid that there will be no one to come after them, because even if good players come in the future, but there is no one to fight against, it is difficult to elicit their wonderful and subtle points. In short, their decision to come and show their skills is enough to make us open our eyes, and their outstanding skills make you applaud and exclaim automatically, thinking that it is the highest peak of art.

Zhejiang Literature Exhibition Extended by Three Days; Closes on the 18th; Special Exhibition of Cultural Relics of Zhang Taiyan

(Hangzhou Correspondence) The Zhejiang Provincial Library is holding the Zhejiang Literature Exhibition, which collects and displays books and cultural relics from all over Zhejiang, which are very beautiful and rich. The exhibition started on November 1st, and many people from this province and other places have come to visit. The grand occasion has been reported in various newspapers. Now it is learned that the exhibition date was originally scheduled for about half a month, and it will close on the 15th. Now, in response to the enthusiastic visits from all parties and the requests from visitors from afar, it has been decided to extend the exhibition for three days, until the 18th (Wednesday). The exhibition is divided into twelve exhibition rooms, including calligraphy and paintings, manuscripts, transcriptions, meticulously engraved portraits, antiques, bronze and stone rubbings, and revolutionary literature of various types. They are classified and displayed with explanations, and special publications of key items are distributed. The location is on Daxue Road, Hangzhou. In addition, since the memorial service for Mr. Zhang Taiyan was initiated in the provincial capital, it will be held in the library. In order to commend the former Confucian and provide observation for future generations, the library has specially opened a cultural relics exhibition room of Mr. Zhang, collecting Mr. Zhang's portraits, posthumous works, ink writings, and objects (such as pens, walking sticks, etc.), a total of dozens of types and more than one hundred pieces. In addition to Mr. Zhang's friends, most of them were borrowed from Mr. Zhang's family and the Zhang's National Studies Association from Su Yunlai, which is very rare. The exhibition will start on the 13th, which is also expected to be welcomed by people from other places who admire Mr. Zhang.

Measures for Primary and Secondary School Teachers and Staff to Attend Academic Lectures; The Municipal Social Bureau Announced It Yesterday for Public Knowledge

The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau and the China Society for Arts and Sciences are jointly holding academic lectures in order to assist teachers and staff in further studies. The measures have been reported in yesterday's newspaper. Now, the interim measures for primary and secondary school teachers and staff to attend academic lectures are reported as follows: (1) The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau (hereinafter referred to as the Bureau) is jointly holding academic lectures with the China Society for Arts and Sciences in order to assist the teachers and staff of the primary and secondary schools and various institutions under its jurisdiction in further studies. All teachers and staff of public and private primary and secondary schools and various institutions under the Bureau's jurisdiction shall attend lectures in accordance with these measures. (2) A total of four academic lectures will be held in the first semester of the 25th year. Each teacher and staff member of the primary and secondary schools and various institutions under the Bureau's jurisdiction must attend at least one session. (3) The teachers and staff members of the primary and secondary schools and various institutions under the Bureau's jurisdiction who attend academic lectures shall be selected by the principals of each school or the administrative heads of each institution in an average rotation, with the principle that the number of attendees at each session accounts for one-quarter of the total number of people. (4) If the number of teachers and staff members of the primary and secondary schools and various institutions under the Bureau's jurisdiction is less than four, the principals of each school or the administrative heads of each institution shall also rotate and select attendees to meet the requirements of Article 2 of these measures that each person attend at least one session. (5) When teachers and staff members of the primary and secondary schools and various institutions under the Bureau's jurisdiction attend academic lectures, they shall sign in at the location designated by the Bureau, and shall not sign in on behalf of others. If necessary, the Bureau may send personnel to check the attendance. (6) Teachers and staff members of the primary and secondary schools and various institutions under the Bureau's jurisdiction who attend academic lectures shall arrive 30 minutes before the start of the lecture, abide by the order of the venue, and shall not leave early in the middle of the lecture. (7) Teachers and staff members of the primary and secondary schools and various institutions under the Bureau's jurisdiction who attend academic lectures shall report what they have learned to the teachers and staff who have not attended at any time. (8) The number and names of teachers and staff members of the primary and secondary schools and various institutions under the Bureau's jurisdiction who attend academic lectures shall be recorded by the Bureau for each session, and shall be reviewed and verified at the end of the semester. Those who have never attended throughout the semester may be given appropriate punishment. (7) The expenses for teachers and staff members of the primary and secondary schools and various institutions under the Bureau's jurisdiction to attend academic lectures shall be borne by the teachers and staff themselves. (10) These measures shall be formulated and promulgated by the Bureau and implemented.
